Technical O
Description O
Proof O
of O
Concept O
Code O
Ston3D O
is O
a O
cross-platform O
technology O
allowing O

developed O
with O
ShiVa O
product O
to O

run O
from O

media O
, O
such O
as O
a O

, O

or O
interactive O
equipment O
. O

This O
can O
be O
